## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate Conv2D kernel in /workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p56/optimization_rounds/round1/output_model_new.py

  MFMA invariants:
  - Keep the block tile fixed at `128 x 128`.
  - Interpret the 4 warps as a fixed `2 x 2` warp grid:
  - Keep the MFMA work per warp fixed at a `64 x 64` tile built as a `2 x 2` array of `32 x 32` MFMA tiles.

  Operand-fragment invariants:
  - Use:
    - `lane_col = lane % 32`
    - `lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4`
  - Advance K in MFMA-sized chunks:
    - `k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e`, where `e in [0, 4)`
  - For A, for each warp-row subtile `tm in [0, 2)`:
    - `m = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32 + lane_col`
    - `a_frag[tm, e]` is the 4-element BF16 fragment for that `(m, k:k+4)` slice
  - For B, for each warp-col subtile `tn in [0, 2)`:
    - `n = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32 + lane_col`
    - `b_frag[tn, e]` is the 4-element BF16 fragment for that `(k:k+4, n)` slice
  - Do not invent a different swizzle, lane permutation, or fragment packing rule.

  Accumulator invariants:
  - Keep one MFMA accumulator per `32 x 32` subtile:
    - `acc[tm, tn] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[tm], b_frag[tn], acc[tm, tn])`
  - Build the per-warp `64 x 64` tile only by applying the fixed subtile offsets `tm * 32` and `tn * 32`.
  - Build the full block tile only by applying the fixed warp-grid offsets `warp_row * 64` and `warp_col * 64`.

  Writeback invariants:
  - The MFMA accumulator layout is fixed and must be unpacked exactly as:
    - `tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32`
    - `tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32`
    - `col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)`
    - `row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)`
  - Fixed mapping:
    - `acc[tm, tn, acc_idx] -> output(row, col)`
  - Do not use a contiguous `acc_idx -> row` mapping.

  Scope invariants:
  - This is an MFMA-only transformation.
  - Do not add LDS staging, vectorized loads, async copies, or a different tile shape as part of this change.
  - Preserve the supported behavior of the existing kernel.
  - Do not look at other commits in the repo.

  Update callsites:
  - /workspace/substrate/test/examples/conv2d/amdgpu/test_conv2d_asym.py
  - /workspace/substrate/benchmark/conv2d/bench_conv2d.py

- Make the optimized path cudagraph-safe: never build descriptor / metadata device tensors inside `forward()`. Prebuild or cache them and reuse them; only rebuild if the underlying storage pointer changes.
- Do not use torch native compute anywhere in `output_model_new.py` to perform convolution, multiplication, or linear algebra, including fallback branches.
- The optimized kernel must actually issue MFMA instructions in the substrate kernel; a solution that does not use MFMA is not acceptable.

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import importlib.util
import unittest
import _substrate_bindings as _C
import torch

from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


ROUND_OUTPUT = "/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p55/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round2/output_model_new.py"


def _load_round_module():
    spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("kb_round2_output_model_new", ROUND_OUTPUT)
    if spec is None or spec.loader is None:
        raise RuntimeError(f"Unable to load round module from {ROUND_OUTPUT}.")
    module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
    spec.loader.exec_module(module)
    return module


def _generate_mlir(jit_fn) -> str:
    jit_deps = _collect_jit_dependencies(jit_fn)
    import_module = _build_import_module([jit_fn, *jit_deps])

    generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
    generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)

    for dep in jit_deps:
        dep_func = _get_function_def(dep.parse())
        generator.visit_function_def(dep_func, "[]", "jit")

    kernel_func = _get_function_def(jit_fn.parse())
    generator.visit_function_def(kernel_func, "[]", "kernel")
    return generator.get_mlir()


@unittest.skipUnless(has_rocm(), "Requires ROCm/HIP with an AMD GPU.")
class TestConv2DAsym(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_weight_cache_reuses_device_tensor_until_storage_changes(self):
        module = _load_round_module()
        model = module.ModelNew(64, 128, 3, stride=1, padding=0, dilation=1, groups=1, bias=False).cuda()
        x = torch.empty(module.INPUT0_SHAPE, dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")

        with torch.no_grad():
            cached0 = model._get_cached_weight(x)
            cached1 = model._get_cached_weight(x)
            self.assertEqual(cached0.data_ptr(), cached1.data_ptr())

            model.conv2d.weight = torch.nn.Parameter(model.conv2d.weight.detach().clone())
            cached2 = model._get_cached_weight(x)
            self.assertNotEqual(cached1.data_ptr(), cached2.data_ptr())

    def test_kernel_mlir_contains_mfma(self):
        module = _load_round_module()
        mlir = _generate_mlir(module.fused_kernel)
        self.assertIn("mfma", mlir)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S

def _launch():
    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
INPUT0_SHAPE = (8, 64, 512, 256)
OUTPUT_SHAPE = (8, 128, 508, 250)
WEIGHT_SHAPE = (128, 64, 5, 7)

@substrate.jit
def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 256), S.f32), W: S.Tensor((128, 64, 5, 7), S.f32), Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 508, 250), S.f32)):
    for n in S.range(8):
        for oc in S.range(128):
            for o0 in S.range(508):
                for o1 in S.range(250):
                    acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
                    g = oc // 128
                    ic_base = g * 64
                    for ic_local in S.range(64):
                        ic = ic_base + ic_local
                        for k0 in S.range(5):
                            for k1 in S.range(7):
                                i0 = o0 * 1 - 0 + k0 * 1
                                i1 = o1 * 1 - 0 + k1 * 1
                                if (i0 >= 0 and i0 < 512) and (i1 >= 0 and i1 < 256):
                                    acc += S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.f32) * S.convert(W[oc, ic_local, k0, k1], S.f32)
                    Y[n, oc, o0, o1] = acc

class ModelNew(nn.Module):

    def __init__(self, in_channels: int, out_channels: int, kernel_size: tuple, stride: tuple = (1, 1), padding: tuple = (0, 0), dilation: tuple = (1, 1), groups: int = 1, bias: bool = False):
            super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
            self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size, stride=stride, padding=padding, dilation=dilation, groups=groups, bias=bias)

    def forward(self, x):
        if tuple(x.shape) != (8, 64, 512, 256) or x.dtype != torch.float32:
            raise RuntimeError('This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.')
        x0 = x.contiguous()
        w = self.conv2d.weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        y = torch.empty((8, 128, 508, 250), device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
        fused_kernel[_launch](x0, w, y)
        return y

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Conv2D benchmark for the current optimization-round kernel."""
import argparse
import importlib.util
from pathlib import Path

import torch


ROUND_DIR = Path("/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p55/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round2")
KERNEL_PATH = ROUND_DIR / "output_model_new.py"


def _load_kernel_module():
    spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("kb_round2_output_model_new", KERNEL_PATH)
    if spec is None or spec.loader is None:
        raise RuntimeError(f"Unable to load kernel module from {KERNEL_PATH}.")
    module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
    spec.loader.exec_module(module)
    return module


kernel_module = _load_kernel_module()


def _ensure_rocm_available(label):
    """Check that ROCm/HIP is available."""
    if not torch.cuda.is_available():
        raise RuntimeError("CUDA is not available.")
    if not hasattr(torch.version, "hip") or torch.version.hip is None:
        raise RuntimeError(f"HIP is not available; {label} benchmark requires ROCm.")


def run_conv2d_benchmark(
    batch_size,
    in_channels,
    out_channels,
    kernel_h,
    kernel_w,
    in_h,
    in_w,
    warmup,
    repeat,
    iters,
    validate,
):
    """
    Run conv2d benchmark.

    Args:
        batch_size: Batch size of input tensor
        in_channels: Number of input channels
        out_channels: Number of output channels
        kernel_h: Height of convolution kernel
        kernel_w: Width of convolution kernel
        in_h: Height of input image
        in_w: Width of input image
        warmup: Number of warmup iterations
        repeat: Number of benchmark repeats
        iters: Number of graph replays per timing repeat
        validate: Whether to validate output correctness
    """
    _ensure_rocm_available("conv2d_round2")

    # Compute output dimensions
    stride_h = stride_w = 1
    dilation = 1
    padding = 0

    out_h = (in_h + 2 * padding - dilation * (kernel_h - 1) - 1) // stride_h + 1
    out_w = (in_w + 2 * padding - dilation * (kernel_w - 1) - 1) // stride_w + 1

    # Create input tensors
    input = torch.randn((batch_size, in_channels, in_h, in_w), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
    weight = torch.randn((out_channels, in_channels, kernel_h, kernel_w), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")

    model = kernel_module.ModelNew(
        in_channels,
        out_channels,
        kernel_h,
        stride=stride_h,
        padding=padding,
        dilation=dilation,
        groups=1,
        bias=False,
    ).cuda()
    with torch.no_grad():
        model.conv2d.weight.copy_(weight)
        model._get_cached_weight(input)

    out = torch.empty((batch_size, out_channels, out_h, out_w), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")

    for _ in range(warmup):
        out.copy_(model(input))
    torch.cuda.synchronize()

    graph = torch.cuda.CUDAGraph()
    capture_stream = torch.cuda.Stream()
    with torch.cuda.graph(graph, stream=capture_stream):
        out.copy_(model(input))
    torch.cuda.synchronize()

    start_evt = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
    end_evt = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
    start_evt.record()
    for _ in range(repeat):
        for _ in range(iters):
            graph.replay()
    end_evt.record()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()

    elapsed_ms = start_evt.elapsed_time(end_evt)
    elapsed = (elapsed_ms * 1.0e-3) / (repeat * iters)

    flops_per_output = in_channels * kernel_h * kernel_w * 2  # mul + add
    total_flops = batch_size * out_channels * out_h * out_w * flops_per_output
    tflops = total_flops / elapsed / 1.0e12

    input_bytes = batch_size * in_channels * in_h * in_w * 4
    weight_bytes = out_channels * in_channels * kernel_h * kernel_w * 4
    output_bytes = batch_size * out_channels * out_h * out_w * 4
    bytes_moved = input_bytes + weight_bytes + output_bytes
    bandwidth = bytes_moved / elapsed / 1.0e9

    print(
        f"batch={batch_size} in_c={in_channels} out_c={out_channels} "
        f"kernel=({kernel_h},{kernel_w}) in=({in_h},{in_w}) out=({out_h},{out_w}) "
        f"time_ms={elapsed * 1.0e3:.4f} tflops={tflops:.3f} bandwidth_gbs={bandwidth:.3f}"
    )

    if validate:
        expected = torch.nn.functional.conv2d(input, weight, stride=(stride_h, stride_w), padding=padding, dilation=dilation)
        actual = out
        max_abs = torch.max(torch.abs(actual - expected)).item()
        if not torch.allclose(actual, expected, rtol=1e-4, atol=1e-4):
            raise AssertionError(f"Validation failed (max abs diff {max_abs}).")
        print(f"validation=max_abs_diff:{max_abs:.6f}")


def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        description="AMDGPU Conv2D benchmark for the current round kernel"
    )
    parser.add_argument("--batch_size", type=int, default=8, help="Batch size")
    parser.add_argument("--in_channels", type=int, default=64, help="Number of input channels")
    parser.add_argument("--out_channels", type=int, default=128, help="Number of output channels")
    parser.add_argument("--kernel_h", type=int, default=3, help="Kernel height")
    parser.add_argument("--kernel_w", type=int, default=3, help="Kernel width")
    parser.add_argument("--in_h", type=int, default=512, help="Input image height")
    parser.add_argument("--in_w", type=int, default=1024, help="Input image width")
    parser.add_argument("--warmup", type=int, default=10, help="Number of warmup iterations")
    parser.add_argument("--repeat", type=int, default=100, help="Number of benchmark repeats")
    parser.add_argument("--iters", type=int, default=100, help="Graph replays per timing repeat")
    parser.add_argument("--validate", action="store_true", default=False, help="Validate output correctness")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    run_conv2d_benchmark(
        batch_size=args.batch_size,
        in_channels=args.in_channels,
        out_channels=args.out_channels,
        kernel_h=args.kernel_h,
        kernel_w=args.kernel_w,
        in_h=args.in_h,
        in_w=args.in_w,
        warmup=args.warmup,
        repeat=args.repeat,
        iters=args.iters,
        validate=args.validate,
    )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_16x16x16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane

 succeeded in 0ms:
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import argparse

import torch

from substrate_kernels import amdgpu_gemm

def _ensure_rocm_available(label):
    if not torch.cuda.is_available():
        raise RuntimeError("CUDA is not available.")
    if not hasattr(torch.version, "hip") or torch.version.hip is None:
        raise RuntimeError(f"HIP is not available; {label} benchmark requires ROCm.")


def run_gemm_pipeline_benchmark(m, n, k, warmup, repeat, iters, validate, row_major_b):
    _ensure_rocm_available("gemm_1stage")
    amdgpu_gemm.gemm_1stage_validate_shape(m, n, k)

    A = torch.randn((m, k), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
    B = torch.randn((k, n), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
    C = torch.zeros((m, n), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")

    if row_major_b:
        kernel = amdgpu_gemm.gemm_1stage_pipeline_row_major
        kernel_b = B
    else:
        kernel = amdgpu_gemm.gemm_1stage_pipeline_transposed_b
        kernel_b = B.t().contiguous()

    # Warmup to JIT-compile and stabilize clocks.
    for _ in range(warmup):
        kernel(A, kernel_b, C)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()

    # Capture the kernel launch in a CUDAGraph for low-overhead replays.
    graph = torch.cuda.CUDAGraph()
    capture_stream = torch.cuda.Stream()
    with torch.cuda.graph(graph, stream=capture_stream):
        kernel(A, kernel_b, C)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()

    start_evt = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
    end_evt = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
    start_evt.record()
    for _ in range(repeat):
        for _ in range(iters):
            graph.replay()
    end_evt.record()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    elapsed_ms = start_evt.elapsed_time(end_evt)
    elapsed = (elapsed_ms * 1.0e-3) / (repeat * iters)

    flops = 2.0 * m * n * k
    tflops = flops / elapsed / 1.0e12

    bytes_moved = (m * k + k * n + m * n) * 2
    bandwidth = bytes_moved / elapsed / 1.0e9

    print(f"M={m} N={n} K={k} time_ms={elapsed * 1.0e3:.4f} tflops={tflops:.3f} bandwidth_gbs={bandwidth:.3f}")

    if validate:
        expected = (A @ B).to(dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cpu")
        actual = C.to("cpu")
        max_abs = torch.max(torch.abs(actual - expected)).item()
        if not torch.allclose(actual, expected, rtol=1e-2, atol=1e-3):
            raise AssertionError(f"Validation failed (max abs diff {max_abs}).")
        print(f"validation=max_abs_diff:{max_abs:.6f}")


def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        description="AMDGPU GEMM pipeline benchmark (M,N multiples of 128; K multiple of 64)"
    )
    parser.add_argument("--m", type=int, default=128)
    parser.add_argument("--n", type=int, default=128)
    parser.add_argument("--k", type=int, default=64)
    parser.add_argument("--warmup", type=int, default=10)
    parser.add_argument("--repeat", type=int, default=100)
    parser.add_argument("--iters", type=int, default=100, help="Graph replays per timing repeat")
    parser.add_argument("--validate", action="store_true", default=False)
    parser.add_argument(
        "--row-major-b",
        action="store_true",
        default=False,
        help="Benchmark the row-major B[k, n] kernel instead of the default pre-transposed B[n, k] kernel",
    )
    args = parser.parse_args()

    run_gemm_pipeline_benchmark(
        args.m, args.n, args.k, args.warmup, args.repeat, args.iters, args.validate, args.row_major_b
    )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
import _substrate_bindings as _C
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip(
    src: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    dst: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)
    dst_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(dst, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    offset_x2 = S.convert(4, S.i32)
    offset_x4 = S.convert(12, S.i32)

    value_x1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x1(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    value_x2 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x2(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    value_x4 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)

    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x1(value_x1, dst_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x2(value_x2, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x4(value_x4, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view(
    src: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    dst: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    frag = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    for i in S.range(2):
        for j in S.range(4):
            dst[i * 4 + j] = frag[i, j, 0]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_buffer_atomic_add_f32(
    target: S.Tensor((1,), S.f32),
    delta: S.Tensor((1,), S.f32),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(target, range_bytes)
    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    S.amdgpu.buffer_atomic_add_f32(delta[0], rsrc, zero, zero, 0)


def generate_mlir(jit_fn) -> str:
    jit_deps = _collect_jit_dependencies(jit_fn)
    import_module = _build_import_module([jit_fn, *jit_deps])

    generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
    generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)

    for dep in jit_deps:
        dep_func = _get_function_def(dep.parse())
        generator.visit_function_def(dep_func, "[]", "jit")

    kernel_func = _get_function_def(jit_fn.parse())
    generator.visit_function_def(kernel_func, "[]", "kernel")
    return generator.get_mlir()


@unittest.skipUnless(
    has_rocm(),
    "Requires ROCm/HIP with an AMD GPU.",
)
class TestAMDGPUBufferOps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_raw_buffer_roundtrip(self):
        src = torch.arange(7, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") * 17 - 9
        dst = torch.full((7,), -1, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_make_rsrc_generates_pointer_and_range(self):
        mlir = generate_mlir(kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip)

        self.assertIn(
            "substrate.memref.extract_aligned_pointer_as_index",
            mlir,
        )
        self.assertGreaterEqual(mlir.count("vector.insert %arg2"), 2, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_load"), 3, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_store"), 3, mlir)

    def test_raw_buffer_bf16_view_extract(self):
        src = torch.randn((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        dst = torch.zeros((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_buffer_atomic_add_f32_updates_target(self):
        target = torch.tensor([1.5], dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
        delta = torch.tensor([2.25], dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = target.numel() * target.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_buffer_atomic_add_f32[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            target, delta, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.allclose(target.cpu(), torch.tensor([3.75], dtype=torch.float32))
        )

    def test_buffer_atomic_add_f32_generates_rocdl_op(self):
        mlir = generate_mlir(kernel_amdgpu_buffer_atomic_add_f32)

        self.assertIn(
            "rocdl.raw.buffer.atomic.fadd",
            mlir,
        )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


@substrate.jit
def kernel_full_1d_i32(
    output_data: S.Tensor((4,), S.i32),
):
    ones = S.full((4,), 1, S.i32)
    for i in S.range(4):
        output_data[i] = ones[i]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_full_2d_f32(
    output_data: S.Tensor((2, 4), S.f32),
):
    acc = S.full((2, 4), 0.0, S.f32)
    for i in S.range(2):
        for j in S.range(4):
            output_data[i, j] = acc[i, j]
            
@substrate.jit
def kernel_full_vector(
    output_data: S.Tensor((1, 4), S.u32),
):
    ones = S.full((1, 4), 1, S.u32)
    output_data[0] = ones[0]


class TestFullTensor(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_full_1d_i32(self):
        """Test substrate.full with 1D i32 tensor filled with 1s"""
        output_data = torch.zeros((4,), dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        expected = torch.full((4,), 1, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")

        kernel_full_1d_i32[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](output_data)

        actual = output_data.cpu()
        expected = expected.cpu()

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(actual, expected),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {actual.tolist()}",
        )

        print("\n1D Full Result (i32, first element filled with 1): \n", actual)

    def test_full_2d_f32(self):
        """Test substrate.full with 2D f32 tensor filled with 0.0"""
        output_data = torch.zeros((2, 4), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
        expected = torch.zeros((2, 4), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")

        kernel_full_2d_f32[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](output_data)

        actual = output_data.cpu()
        expected = expected.cpu()

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(actual, expected),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {actual.tolist()}",
        )

        print("\n2D Full Result (f32, filled with 0.0): \n", actual)
        
    def test_full_vector(self):
        """Test substrate.full with 1D vector tensor filled with 1s"""
        output_data = torch.zeros((1, 4), dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        expected = torch.full((1, 4), 1, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")

        kernel_full_vector[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](output_data)

        actual = output_data.cpu()
        expected = expected.cpu()

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(actual, expected),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {actual.tolist()}",
        )

        print("\n1D Vector Full Result (i32, first element filled with 1): \n", actual)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
import _substrate_bindings as _C
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)


@substrate.jit
def kernel_scalar_assign(out: S.Tensor((8,), S.i32)):
    base = S.convert(7, S.i32)
    for i in S.range(8):
        out[i] = base + i


@substrate.jit
def kernel_vector_row_assign(
    out: S.Tensor((2, 4), S.u32),
    src: S.Tensor((2, 4), S.u32),
):
    row = src[0]
    row[2] = S.convert(99, S.u32)
    out[0] = row
    out[1] = src[1]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_memcpy(
    dst: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    src: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
):
    thread_id = S.thread_id(0)
    dst[thread_id] = src[thread_id]


class TestTensorAssignments(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_scalar_assignment(self):
        out = torch.zeros((8,), dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        expected = torch.arange(8, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") + 7

        kernel_scalar_assign[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](out)

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(out.cpu(), expected.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {out.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_vector_row_assignment(self):
        src = torch.arange(2 * 4, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda").view(2, 4)
        out = torch.zeros((2, 4), dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")

        kernel_vector_row_assign[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](out, src)

        expected = src.clone()
        expected[0, 2] = 99

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(out.cpu(), expected.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {out.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_vector_memcpy(self):
        src = torch.arange(64 * 4, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda").view(64, 4)
        dst = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")

        kernel_memcpy[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](dst, src)

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_vector_memcpy_mlir_uses_load_vec(self):
        jit_deps = _collect_jit_dependencies(kernel_memcpy)
        import_module = _build_import_module([kernel_memcpy, *jit_deps])

        generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
        generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)

        for dep in jit_deps:
            dep_func = _get_function_def(dep.parse())
            generator.visit_function_def(dep_func, "[]", "jit")

        kernel_func = _get_function_def(kernel_memcpy.parse())
        generator.visit_function_def(kernel_func, "[]", "kernel")

        mlir = generator.get_mlir()
        self.assertIn("substrate.memref.load_vec", mlir)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import _substrate_bindings as _C
import substrate
import substrate.language as S

from substrate.compiler import code_generator as cg
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.compiler.compiler import ASTSource


@substrate.jit
def kernel_with_num_warps(
    x: S.Tensor((1,), S.i32),
    BLOCK_SIZE: S.constexpr,
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    if tid < BLOCK_SIZE:
        x[tid] = x[tid]


class TestNumWarps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_amdgpu_llvm_ir_overrides_flat_workgroup_size_when_num_warps_set(self):
        src = ASTSource(
            kernel_with_num_warps,
            {"x": "*i32", "BLOCK_SIZE": "constexpr"},
            constexprs={"BLOCK_SIZE": {"type": "i32", "value": 16}},
        )
        constexprs_json = cg._serialize_constexprs(src)

        generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
        import_module = _build_import_module(
            [kernel_with_num_warps, *_collect_jit_dependencies(kernel_with_num_warps)]
        )
        generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)
        generator.visit_function_def(
            _get_function_def(kernel_with_num_warps.parse()), constexprs_json, "kernel"
        )

        llvm_ir = generator.get_llvm_ir("amdgcn-amd-amdhsa", "gfx90a", 2, 3)
        self.assertIn('"amdgpu-flat-work-group-size"="1,192"', llvm_ir)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor(INPUT0_SHAPE, S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((K_FLAT, OUT_CHANNELS), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor(OUTPUT_SHAPE, S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // 8):
+        a_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            m = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + tm * 32 + lane_col
+            if m < M_FLAT:
+                batch = m // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                out_idx = m % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0 = out_idx // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_idx % OUT_W
+
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    ic = k // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                    kernel_idx = k % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                    k0 = kernel_idx // KERNEL_W
+                    k1 = kernel_idx % KERNEL_W
+                    a_frag[tm, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch, ic, o0 + k0, o1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            n = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + tn * 32 + lane_col
+            if n < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    b_frag[tn, e, 0] = W[k, n]
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            for tn in S.range(2):
+                acc[tm, tn] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[tm], b_frag[tn], acc[tm, tn])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + tm * 32
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < M_FLAT:
+                        batch = row // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                        out_idx = row % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                        o0 = out_idx // OUT_W
+                        o1 = out_idx % OUT_W
+                        Y[batch, col, o0, o1] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]
+

+    def _pack_weight(self, weight: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        if tuple(weight.shape) != WEIGHT_SHAPE:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark weight shape.")
+        return weight.permute(1, 2, 3, 0).contiguous().view(K_FLAT, OUT_CHANNELS).to(dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+
+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:

+        storage_ptr = weight.untyped_storage().data_ptr()

+        if (
+            self._cached_weight is None
+            or self._cached_weight_ptr != storage_ptr
+            or self._cached_weight_device != device
+        ):
+            weight_dev = weight.detach().to(device=device, dtype=torch.float32).contiguous()

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor(INPUT0_SHAPE, S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((K_FLAT, OUT_CHANNELS), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor(OUTPUT_SHAPE, S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // 8):
+        a_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            m = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + tm * 32 + lane_col
+            if m < M_FLAT:
+                batch = m // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                out_idx = m % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0 = out_idx // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_idx % OUT_W
+
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    ic = k // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                    kernel_idx = k % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                    k0 = kernel_idx // KERNEL_W
+                    k1 = kernel_idx % KERNEL_W
+                    a_frag[tm, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch, ic, o0 + k0, o1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            n = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + tn * 32 + lane_col
+            if n < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    b_frag[tn, e, 0] = W[k, n]
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            for tn in S.range(2):
+                acc[tm, tn] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[tm], b_frag[tn], acc[tm, tn])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + tm * 32
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < M_FLAT:
+                        batch = row // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                        out_idx = row % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                        o0 = out_idx // OUT_W
+                        o1 = out_idx % OUT_W
+                        Y[batch, col, o0, o1] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]
+

+                        batch = row // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                        out_idx = row % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                        o0 = out_idx // OUT_W
+                        o1 = out_idx % OUT_W
+                        Y[batch, col, o0, o1] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]
+

+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,

+        bias: bool = False,

+        if tuple(weight.shape) != WEIGHT_SHAPE:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark weight shape.")
+        return weight.permute(1, 2, 3, 0).contiguous().view(K_FLAT, OUT_CHANNELS).to(dtype=torch.bfloat16)

+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight
+        storage_ptr = weight.untyped_storage().data_ptr()

+        if (
+            self._cached_weight is None
+            or self._cached_weight_ptr != storage_ptr
+            or self._cached_weight_device != device
+        ):
+            weight_dev = weight.detach().to(device=device, dtype=torch.float32).contiguous()

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 256), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((2240, 128), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 508, 250), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // 8):
+        a_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            m = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + tm * 32 + lane_col
+            if m < M_FLAT:
+                batch = m // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                out_idx = m % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0 = out_idx // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_idx % OUT_W
+
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    ic = k // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                    kernel_idx = k % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                    k0 = kernel_idx // KERNEL_W
+                    k1 = kernel_idx % KERNEL_W
+                    a_frag[tm, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch, ic, o0 + k0, o1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            n = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + tn * 32 + lane_col
+            if n < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    b_frag[tn, e, 0] = W[k, n]
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            for tn in S.range(2):
+                acc[tm, tn] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[tm], b_frag[tn], acc[tm, tn])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + tm * 32
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):

+                    if row < M_FLAT:

+                        out_idx = row % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                        o0 = out_idx // OUT_W
+                        o1 = out_idx % OUT_W
+                        Y[batch, col, o0, o1] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]

-                    Y[n, oc, o0, o1] = acc
+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 256), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((2240, 128), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 508, 250), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // 8):
+        a_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            m = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + tm * 32 + lane_col
+            if m < M_FLAT:
+                batch = m // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                out_idx = m % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0 = out_idx // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_idx % OUT_W
+
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    ic = k // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                    kernel_idx = k % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                    k0 = kernel_idx // KERNEL_W
+                    k1 = kernel_idx % KERNEL_W
+                    a_frag[tm, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch, ic, o0 + k0, o1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            n = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + tn * 32 + lane_col
+            if n < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    b_frag[tn, e, 0] = W[k, n]
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            for tn in S.range(2):
+                acc[tm, tn] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[tm], b_frag[tn], acc[tm, tn])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + tm * 32
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < OUT_CHANNELS:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < M_FLAT:
+                        batch = row // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                        out_idx = row % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                        o0 = out_idx // OUT_W
+                        o1 = out_idx % OUT_W
+                        Y[batch, col, o0, o1] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]
+
 
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=(1, 1),
+        padding=(0, 0),
+        dilation=(1, 1),
+        groups: int = 1,
+        bias: bool = False,
+    ):
+        super().__init__()
+        if isinstance(kernel_size, int):
+            kernel_size = (kernel_size, kernel_size)
+        if isinstance(stride, int):
+            stride = (stride, stride)
+        if isinstance(padding, int):
+            padding = (padding, padding)
+        if isinstance(dilation, int):
+            dilation = (dilation, dilation)
 
-    def __init__(self, in_channels: int, out_channels: int, kernel_size: tuple, stride: tuple = (1, 1), padding: tuple = (0, 0), dilation: tuple = (1, 1), groups: int = 1, bias: bool = False):
-            super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
-            self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size, stride=stride, padding=padding, dilation=dilation, groups=groups, bias=bias)

+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._cached_weight_ptr = None
+        self._cached_weight_device = None
+        self._cached_weight = None
+
+    def _pack_weight(self, weight: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        if tuple(weight.shape) != WEIGHT_SHAPE:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark weight shape.")
+        return weight.permute(1, 2, 3, 0).contiguous().view(K_FLAT, OUT_CHANNELS).to(dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+
+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight
+        storage_ptr = weight.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        device = x.device
+        if (
+            self._cached_weight is None
+            or self._cached_weight_ptr != storage_ptr
+            or self._cached_weight_device != device
+        ):
+            weight_dev = weight.detach().to(device=device, dtype=torch.float32).contiguous()
+            self._cached_weight = self._pack_weight(weight_dev)
+            self._cached_weight_ptr = storage_ptr
+            self._cached_weight_device = device
+        return self._cached_weight
 
     def forward(self, x):

+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")
+        if (
+            self.conv2d.in_channels != IN_CHANNELS
+            or self.conv2d.out_channels != OUT_CHANNELS
+            or self.conv2d.kernel_size != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)

+            or self.conv2d.padding != (0, 0)
+            or self.conv2d.dilation != (1, 1)
+            or self.conv2d.groups != 1
+            or self.conv2d.bias is not None
+        ):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark convolution parameters.")
+
+        w = self._get_cached_weight(x)
+        y = torch.empty(OUTPUT_SHAPE, device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+        fused_kernel[_launch](x, w, y)
         return y

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 256), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((2240, 128), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 508, 250), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_FLAT // 8):
+        a_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            m = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + tm * 32 + lane_col
+            if m < M_FLAT:
+                batch = m // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                out_idx = m % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                o0 = out_idx // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_idx % OUT_W
+
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    ic = k // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                    kernel_idx = k % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)

+                    k1 = kernel_idx % KERNEL_W
+                    a_frag[tm, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch, ic, o0 + k0, o1 + k1], S.bf16)
+

+            if n < OUT_CHANNELS:

+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + tm * 32
+        for tn in S.range(2):

+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < OUT_CHANNELS:

+                        o0 = out_idx // OUT_W

+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,

+        bias: bool = False,

+        )

+    def _pack_weight(self, weight: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        if tuple(weight.shape) != WEIGHT_SHAPE:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark weight shape.")
+        return weight.permute(1, 2, 3, 0).contiguous().view(K_FLAT, OUT_CHANNELS).to(dtype=torch.bfloat16)

+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight
+        storage_ptr = weight.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        device = x.device
+        if (
+            self._cached_weight is None
+            or self._cached_weight_ptr != storage_ptr
+            or self._cached_weight_device != device
+        ):
+            weight_dev = weight.detach().to(device=device, dtype=torch.float32).contiguous()

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 256), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((2240, 128), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 508, 250), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(280):
+        a_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            m = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32 + lane_col
+            if m < 1016000:
+                batch = m // 127000
+                out_idx = m % 127000
+                o0 = out_idx // 250
+                o1 = out_idx % 250
+
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    ic = k // 35
+                    kernel_idx = k % 35
+                    k0 = kernel_idx // 7
+                    k1 = kernel_idx % 7
+                    a_frag[tm, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch, ic, o0 + k0, o1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            n = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32 + lane_col
+            if n < 128:
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    b_frag[tn, e, 0] = W[k, n]
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            for tn in S.range(2):
+                acc[tm, tn] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[tm], b_frag[tn], acc[tm, tn])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < 128:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 256), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((2240, 128), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 508, 250), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(280):
+        a_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            m = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32 + lane_col
+            if m < 1016000:
+                batch = m // 127000
+                out_idx = m % 127000
+                o0 = out_idx // 250
+                o1 = out_idx % 250
+
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    ic = k // 35
+                    kernel_idx = k % 35
+                    k0 = kernel_idx // 7
+                    k1 = kernel_idx % 7
+                    a_frag[tm, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch, ic, o0 + k0, o1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            n = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32 + lane_col
+            if n < 128:
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    b_frag[tn, e, 0] = W[k, n]
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            for tn in S.range(2):
+                acc[tm, tn] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[tm], b_frag[tn], acc[tm, tn])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < 128:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < 1016000:
+                        batch = row // 127000
+                        out_idx = row % 127000
+                        o0 = out_idx // 250
+                        o1 = out_idx % 250
+                        Y[batch, col, o0, o1] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]
+

+    def __init__(
+        self,

+    def _pack_weight(self, weight: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        if tuple(weight.shape) != WEIGHT_SHAPE:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark weight shape.")
+        return weight.permute(1, 2, 3, 0).contiguous().view(K_FLAT, OUT_CHANNELS).to(dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+
+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight
+        storage_ptr = weight.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        device = x.device
+        if (
+            self._cached_weight is None
+            or self._cached_weight_ptr != storage_ptr
+            or self._cached_weight_device != device
+        ):

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S


BATCH = 8
IN_CHANNELS = 64
IN_H = 512
IN_W = 256
OUT_CHANNELS = 128
KERNEL_H = 5
KERNEL_W = 7
OUT_H = 508
OUT_W = 250
K_FLAT = IN_CHANNELS * KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W
M_FLAT = BATCH * OUT_H * OUT_W
BLOCK_M = 128
BLOCK_N = 128
WARP_TILE_M = 64
WARP_TILE_N = 64
WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4


def _launch():
    grid_n = (OUT_CHANNELS + BLOCK_N - 1) // BLOCK_N
    grid_m = (M_FLAT + BLOCK_M - 1) // BLOCK_M
    return ((grid_n, grid_m, 1), (WAVES_PER_BLOCK * 64, 1, 1))


INPUT0_SHAPE = (BATCH, IN_CHANNELS, IN_H, IN_W)
OUTPUT_SHAPE = (BATCH, OUT_CHANNELS, OUT_H, OUT_W)
WEIGHT_SHAPE = (OUT_CHANNELS, IN_CHANNELS, KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)


@substrate.jit
def fused_kernel(
    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 256), S.f32),
    W: S.Tensor((2240, 128), S.bf16),
    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 508, 250), S.f32),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    warp_id = tid // 64
    lane = tid % 64

    warp_row = warp_id // 2
    warp_col = warp_id % 2

    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * 128

    lane_col = lane % 32
    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4

    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)

    for k_tile in S.range(280):
        a_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
        b_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)

        for tm in S.range(2):
            m = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32 + lane_col
            if m < 1016000:
                batch = m // 127000
                out_idx = m % 127000
                o0 = out_idx // 250
                o1 = out_idx % 250

                for e in S.range(4):
                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
                    ic = k // 35
                    kernel_idx = k % 35
                    k0 = kernel_idx // 7
                    k1 = kernel_idx % 7
                    a_frag[tm, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch, ic, o0 + k0, o1 + k1], S.bf16)

        for tn in S.range(2):
            n = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32 + lane_col
            if n < 128:
                for e in S.range(4):
                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
                    b_frag[tn, e, 0] = W[k, n]

        for tm in S.range(2):
            for tn in S.range(2):
                acc[tm, tn] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[tm], b_frag[tn], acc[tm, tn])

    for tm in S.range(2):
        tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32
        for tn in S.range(2):
            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32
            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
            if col < 128:
                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
                    if row < 1016000:
                        batch = row // 127000
                        out_idx = row % 127000
                        o0 = out_idx // 250
                        o1 = out_idx % 250
                        Y[batch, col, o0, o1] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(
        self,
        in_channels: int,
        out_channels: int,
        kernel_size,
        stride=(1, 1),
        padding=(0, 0),
        dilation=(1, 1),
        groups: int = 1,
        bias: bool = False,
    ):
        super().__init__()
        if isinstance(kernel_size, int):
            kernel_size = (kernel_size, kernel_size)
        if isinstance(stride, int):
            stride = (stride, stride)
        if isinstance(padding, int):
            padding = (padding, padding)
        if isinstance(dilation, int):
            dilation = (dilation, dilation)

        self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(
            in_channels,
            out_channels,
            kernel_size,
            stride=stride,
            padding=padding,
            dilation=dilation,
            groups=groups,
            bias=bias,
        )
        self._cached_weight_ptr = None
        self._cached_weight_device = None
        self._cached_weight = None

    def _pack_weight(self, weight: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 256), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((2240, 128), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 508, 250), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(280):
+        a_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            m = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32 + lane_col
+            if m < 1016000:
+                batch = m // 127000
+                out_idx = m % 127000
+                o0 = out_idx // 250
+                o1 = out_idx % 250
+
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    ic = k // 35
+                    kernel_idx = k % 35
+                    k0 = kernel_idx // 7
+                    k1 = kernel_idx % 7
+                    a_frag[tm, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch, ic, o0 + k0, o1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            n = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32 + lane_col
+            if n < 128:
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    b_frag[tn, e, 0] = W[k, n]
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            for tn in S.range(2):
+                acc[tm, tn] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[tm], b_frag[tn], acc[tm, tn])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < 128:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < 1016000:
+                        batch = row // 127000
+                        out_idx = row % 127000
+                        o0 = out_idx // 250
+                        o1 = out_idx % 250
+                        Y[batch, col, o0, o1] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 256), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((2240, 128), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 508, 250), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+

+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * 128

+

+        b_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            m = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32 + lane_col
+            if m < 1016000:
+                batch = m // 127000
+                out_idx = m % 127000
+                o0 = out_idx // 250
+                o1 = out_idx % 250

+                    k0 = kernel_idx // 7
+                    k1 = kernel_idx % 7
+                    a_frag[tm, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch, ic, o0 + k0, o1 + k1], S.bf16)

+        tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32
+        for tn in S.range(2):

+                        out_idx = row % 127000
+                        o0 = out_idx // 250
+                        o1 = out_idx % 250

+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 256), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((2240, 128), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 508, 250), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(280):
+        a_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b_frag = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            m = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32 + lane_col
+            if m < 1016000:
+                batch = m // 127000
+                out_idx = m % 127000
+                o0 = out_idx // 250
+                o1 = out_idx % 250
+
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    ic = k // 35
+                    kernel_idx = k % 35
+                    k0 = kernel_idx // 7
+                    k1 = kernel_idx % 7
+                    a_frag[tm, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch, ic, o0 + k0, o1 + k1], S.bf16)
+
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            n = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32 + lane_col
+            if n < 128:
+                for e in S.range(4):
+                    k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+                    b_frag[tn, e, 0] = W[k, n]
+
+        for tm in S.range(2):
+            for tn in S.range(2):
+                acc[tm, tn] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[tm], b_frag[tn], acc[tm, tn])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < 128:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < 1016000:
+                        batch = row // 127000
+                        out_idx = row % 127000
+                        o0 = out_idx // 250
+                        o1 = out_idx % 250
+                        Y[batch, col, o0, o1] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]

Implemented the MFMA-based round1 kernel in [output_model_new.py](/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p56/optimization_rounds/round1/output_model_new.py), with the fixed `128 x 128` block tile, fixed `2 x 2` wave grid, required fragment packing, and the exact accumulator unpack/writeback mapping from the prompt. The optimized path caches the packed device weight outside `forward()` and rebuilds it only when the underlying weight storage pointer changes.

I also updated the round-specific callsites in [test_conv2d_asym.py](/workspace/substrate/test/examples/conv2d/amdgpu/test_conv2d_asym.py) and [bench_conv2d.py](/workspace/substrate/benchmark/conv2d/bench_conv2d.py), and wrote `/workspace/kernel_benchmark/path/to/case.txt` with the current round directory.
